                      <h3 class="Uo8X3b">Description</h3><span>Card Factory is a chain of greeting card and gift stores in the United Kingdom founded in Wakefield by Dean Hoyle and his wife Janet; the first store opened in 1997. It is listed on the London Stock Exchange.</span><span><span> </span><a class="ruhjFe NJLBac fl" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Card_Factory" data-ved="2ahUKEwj5je2158HuAhUATBUIHbdqBDcQmhMwFnoECBoQAg" ping="/url?sa=t&amp;source=web&amp;rct=j&amp;url=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Card_Factory&amp;ved=2ahUKEwj5je2158HuAhUATBUIHbdqBDcQmhMwFnoECBoQAg">Wikipedia</a></span>
                     </div>
                    </div>
